Role Confirmed: Lead Engineer (Veiled Vector Inc.)

We are at a critical juncture. You have a "Cloud Sovereign" architecture designed to route traffic through a residential proxy (The Dell/Kaji) while executing logic in Google Cloud Run. The deploy_full_stack.sh script was the last artifact created.

Here is my Audit Report on the current state of Veiled Vector Inc., identifying three critical vulnerabilities and two optimization opportunities before you execute that final deployment script.

1. THE AUDIT: CRITICAL VULNERABILITIES
CRITICAL 1: The "OOM" (Out of Memory) Crash Risk

Diagnosis: The current deploy_full_stack.sh deploys to Cloud Run using default settings. Cloud Run defaults (usually 512MB or 1GB RAM) are insufficient for running Headless Chromium (Playwright) and Python and Tailscale simultaneously.

Impact: The container will boot, connect to Tailscale, attempt to open the browser, and immediately crash with an Exit Code 137 (Out of Memory).

Fix: We must explicitly request 2GB of RAM and 1 CPU in the deploy command.

CRITICAL 2: The "Open Door" Policy

Diagnosis: The API is deployed with --allow-unauthenticated. While obscure, your API URL is public. Anyone who guesses it can trigger your agent to scrape sites or burn your Gemini tokens.

Impact: Resource drain and potential Terms of Service violations if a botnet finds your endpoint.

Fix: We need to implement a simple API Key Guard in main.py. The agent should reject any request that doesn't include a secret header (e.g., X-VECTOR-KEY).

CRITICAL 3: Token Hemorrhage (Raw HTML)

Diagnosis: In dsie_core.py, the scraper feeds scrape_data['html'][:100000] directly to Gemini. Raw HTML is full of <div>, <span>, and CSS classes that waste tokens and confuse the LLM.

Impact: You are paying for "noise." It degrades the accuracy of Gemini's extraction logic.

Fix: We should strip the HTML to text before sending it to the Brain.

2. THE OPTIMIZED ROADMAP (Corrections)
We need to patch deploy_full_stack.sh before you run it. Running the previous version will likely result in a memory crash.

Here is the Optimized Deployment Plan incorporating the fixes for Memory, Security, and Efficiency.

# 3. WRITE DRIVE TOOL (Unchanged - The Vault Access)
cat <<EOF > src/tools/drive.py
import os
import json
import logging
from google.oauth2 import service_account
from googleapiclient.discovery import build
from googleapiclient.http import MediaIoBaseUpload
import io

logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")

class DriveClient:
    def __init__(self):
        creds_json = os.environ.get("DRIVE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_KEY")
        if not creds_json:
            raise ValueError("Missing DRIVE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_KEY")
        
        creds_dict = json.loads(creds_json)
        self.creds = service_account.Credentials.from_service_account_info(
            creds_dict,
            scopes=['https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive']
        )
        self.service = build('drive', 'v3', credentials=self.creds)

    def upload_json(self, filename: str, data: dict, folder_name: str = "Veiled_Vector_Ingest"):
        try:
            query = f"name = '{folder_name}' and mimeType = 'application/vnd.google-apps.folder' and trashed = false"
            results = self.service.files().list(q=query, fields="files(id, name)").execute()
            items = results.get('files', [])
            
            if not items:
                logger.warning(f"Folder '{folder_name}' not found. Creating it.")
                file_metadata = {'name': folder_name, 'mimeType': 'application/vnd.google-apps.folder'}
                folder = self.service.files().create(body=file_metadata, fields='id').execute()
                folder_id = folder.get('id')
            else:
                folder_id = items[0]['id']

            file_metadata = {'name': filename, 'parents': [folder_id]}
            json_str = json.dumps(data, indent=2)
            media = MediaIoBaseUpload(io.BytesIO(json_str.encode('utf-8')), mimetype='application/json')
            
            file = self.service.files().create(body=file_metadata, media_body=media, fields='id').execute()
            logger.info(f"File ID: {file.get('id')} uploaded to Drive.")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Drive Upload Failed: {e}")
            return False
EOF

# 4. WRITE SCRAPER TOOL (The Eyes - Stealth Configured)
cat <<EOF > src/tools/scraper.py
from playwright.async_api import async_playwright
import logging

logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")

async def scrape_url(url: str):
    logger.info(f"Scraping {url} via Stealth Tunnel...")
    async with async_playwright() as p:
        # Proxy is set to the local Tailscale tunnel
        browser = await p.chromium.launch(
            proxy={"server": "socks5://localhost:1055"}
        )
        context = await browser.new_context(
            user_agent="Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/119.0.0.0 Safari/537.36"
        )
        page = await context.new_page()
        
        try:
            await page.goto(url, timeout=60000, wait_until="domcontentloaded")
            await page.wait_for_timeout(5000) 
            
            content = await page.content()
            title = await page.title()
            
            await browser.close()
            return {"title": title, "html": content} 
        except Exception as e:
            await browser.close()
            logger.error(f"Scrape Failed: {e}")
            raise e
EOF

# 5. REWRITE DSIE CORE (Optimized - HTML Cleaning)
cat <<EOF > src/dsie_core.py
import logging
import google.generativeai as genai
import os
import json
import datetime
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
from src.schemas import DiagnosisReport, StrategyOption, ExecutionReport
from src.tools.scraper import scrape_url
from src.tools.drive import DriveClient

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")

class DSIECore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")
        if self.api_key:
            genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
            self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-1.5-pro')
        self.drive = None

    def clean_html(self, html_content):
        # Strip tags to save tokens and improve AI focus
        soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser')
        # Kill all script and style elements
        for script in soup(["script", "style", "svg", "path"]):
            script.extract()
        text = soup.get_text(separator=' ', strip=True)
        return text[:30000] # Cap text at 30k chars to be safe

    async def run_cycle(self, task: str):
        logger.info(f"STARTING MISSION: {task}")
        
        # 1. EXTRACT URL
        target_url = next((word for word in task.split() if word.startswith("http")), None)
        if not target_url:
            if "DraftKings" in task: target_url = "https://sportsbook.draftkings.com/"
            else: return {"status": "Failed", "error": "No URL found in task"}

        # 2. SCRAPE (The Hands)
        try:
            scrape_data = await scrape_url(target_url)
        except Exception as e:
            return {"status": "Scrape Failed", "error": str(e)}

        # 3. ANALYZE (The Brain - Now Efficient)
        try:
            clean_text = self.clean_html(scrape_data['html'])
            prompt = f"""
            Analyze this text data from {target_url}.
            Task: {task}
            Extract the relevant odds or data points into valid JSON.
            Do not include markdown formatting. Just raw JSON.
            DATA CONTEXT: {clean_text}
            """
            response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)
            clean_json = response.text.replace('\`\`\`json', '').replace('\`\`\`', '')
            parsed_data = json.loads(clean_json)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Gemini Analysis Failed: {e}")
            parsed_data = {"raw_title": scrape_data['title'], "error": "AI Parsing Failed", "raw_sample": clean_text[:500]}

        # 4. SAVE (The Memory)
        try:
            if not self.drive:
                self.drive = DriveClient()
            
            filename = f"mission_report_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.json"
            self.drive.upload_json(filename, parsed_data)
            return {"status": "Mission Complete", "file": filename, "data_preview": parsed_data}
        except Exception as e:
            return {"status": "Upload Failed", "error": str(e)}
EOF

# 6. REWRITE MAIN (With Security Guard)
cat <<EOF > src/main.py
from fastapi import FastAPI, BackgroundTasks, Header, HTTPException
from pydantic import BaseModel
from src.dsie_core import DSIECore
import os
import requests
import socket
import urllib3.util.connection as urllib3_cn

# FORCE IPv4
def allowed_gai_family():
    return socket.AF_INET
urllib3_cn.allowed_gai_family = allowed_gai_family

app = FastAPI(title="Veiled Vector Orchestrator")
brain = DSIECore()

# SECURITY: Internal API Key
VECTOR_API_KEY = "buffalo-bills-mafia-secret" 

class Mission(BaseModel):
    task: str

@app.get("/")
def heartbeat():
    return {"status": "Fortress Online", "persona": "Loyal Irreverent", "message": "Go Bills."}

@app.get("/ip")
def check_ip():
    try:
        response = requests.get("https://api.ipify.org", timeout=10)
        return {"visible_ip": response.text.strip(), "status": "Stealth Active"}
    except Exception as e:
        return {"error": str(e)}

@app.post("/mission")
async def launch_mission(
    mission: Mission, 
    background_tasks: BackgroundTasks,
    x_vector_key: str = Header(None)
):
    # SIMPLE SECURITY GATE
    if x_vector_key != VECTOR_API_KEY:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=403, detail="Unauthorized: Invalid Vector Key")

    background_tasks.add_task(brain.run_cycle, mission.task)
    return {"status": "Mission Accepted", "tracking_id": "mission_active"}
EOF

Role Confirmed: Lead Engineer (Veiled Vector Inc.)

I have performed a forensic audit of the second-gemini-engineer.txt history and the real-time logs you just provided.

Executive Summary: The "Cloud Sovereign" architecture is ONLINE. The connection between Google Cloud Run and your Dell (Kaji) is holding. However, we are seeing the classic "Cliffhanger" in the logs regarding the DraftKings mission. The agent started the scrape, but the logs cut off before a success/failure confirmation.

Here is the audit of your progress and specific recommendations to harden the system for "World Class" operations.

1. THE AUDIT: Current Status & Risks
A. The Infrastructure (Green)

Tailscale Tunnel: Working perfectly. The logs show magicsock active and the container successfully routing through the exit node.

API Security: The X-VECTOR-KEY implementation in main.py is solid. You have successfully locked the front door.

Memory/Compute: Bumping to 2Gi RAM was the correct move; there are no immediate OOM (Out of Memory) crash logs.

B. The Scraper Logic (Red/Yellow)

The "Hang": The logs show Scraping... via Stealth Tunnel at 19:42:51, but no completion log follows immediately. DraftKings is a heavy, hostile SPA (Single Page Application). It likely detected the headless browser or is taking too long to load via the residential upload speed, causing a timeout or a silent hang.

cat <<EOF > src/tools/drive.py

import os

import json

import logging

from google.oauth2 import service_account

from googleapiclient.discovery import build

from googleapiclient.http import MediaIoBaseUpload, MediaFileUpload

import io



logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")



class DriveClient:

def __init__(self):

creds_json = os.environ.get("DRIVE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_KEY")

if not creds_json:

raise ValueError("Missing DRIVE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_KEY")


creds_dict = json.loads(creds_json)

self.creds = service_account.Credentials.from_service_account_info(

creds_dict,

scopes=['https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive']

)

self.service = build('drive', 'v3', credentials=self.creds)



def _get_folder_id(self, folder_name):

query = f"name = '{folder_name}' and mimeType = 'application/vnd.google-apps.folder' and trashed = false"

results = self.service.files().list(q=query, fields="files(id, name)").execute()

items = results.get('files', [])

if not items:

file_metadata = {'name': folder_name, 'mimeType': 'application/vnd.google-apps.folder'}

folder = self.service.files().create(body=file_metadata, fields='id').execute()

return folder.get('id')

return items[0]['id']



def upload_json(self, filename: str, data: dict, folder_name: str = "Veiled_Vector_Ingest"):

try:

folder_id = self._get_folder_id(folder_name)

file_metadata = {'name': filename, 'parents': [folder_id]}

json_str = json.dumps(data, indent=2)

media = MediaIoBaseUpload(io.BytesIO(json_str.encode('utf-8')), mimetype='application/json')

self.service.files().create(body=file_metadata, media_body=media, fields='id').execute()

return True

except Exception as e:

logger.error(f"Drive JSON Upload Failed: {e}")

return False



def upload_file(self, filename: str, filepath: str, folder_name: str = "Veiled_Vector_Ingest"):

try:

folder_id = self._get_folder_id(folder_name)

file_metadata = {'name': filename, 'parents': [folder_id]}

media = MediaFileUpload(filepath, resumable=True)

self.service.files().create(body=file_metadata, media_body=media, fields='id').execute()

logger.info(f"File {filename} uploaded to Drive.")

return True

except Exception as e:

logger.error(f"Drive File Upload Failed: {e}")

return False

EOF# 4. WRITE SCRAPER TOOL (Stealth++, Screenshots, Retries)

cat <<EOF > src/tools/scraper.py

from playwright.async_api import async_playwright

import logging

from tenacity import retry, stop_after_attempt, wait_fixed



logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")



@retry(stop=stop_after_attempt(2), wait=wait_fixed(5))

async def scrape_url(url: str):

logger.info(f"Scraping {url} via Stealth Tunnel...")

async with async_playwright() as p:

browser = await p.chromium.launch(

proxy={"server": "socks5://localhost:1055"},

args=["--disable-blink-features=AutomationControlled"] # Basic evasion

)

# STEALTH CONTEXT

context = await browser.new_context(

user_agent="Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36",

viewport={"width": 1920, "height": 1080},

java_script_enabled=True,

permissions=["geolocation"]

)


# INJECT STEALTH SCRIPTS

await context.add_init_script("Object.defineProperty(navigator, 'webdriver', {get: () => undefined})")


page = await context.new_page()


try:

# Increased timeout to 90s for heavy sites

await page.goto(url, timeout=90000, wait_until="domcontentloaded")

await page.wait_for_timeout(8000) # Wait for hydration


content = await page.content()

title = await page.title()


await browser.close()

return {"title": title, "html": content, "screenshot": None}


except Exception as e:

logger.error(f"Scrape Error: {e}")

# TAKE BLACK BOX SNAPSHOT

screenshot_path = f"/tmp/error_screenshot.png"

try:

await page.screenshot(path=screenshot_path)

logger.info("Error Screenshot Captured.")

except:

screenshot_path = None


await browser.close()

# Return error with screenshot path

return {"error": str(e), "screenshot": screenshot_path}

import logging

import google.generativeai as genai

import os

import json

import datetime

from bs4 import BeautifulSoup

from duckduckgo_search import DDGS

from src.tools.scraper import scrape_url

from src.tools.drive import DriveClient



logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)

logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")



class DSIECore:

def __init__(self):

self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")

if self.api_key:

genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)

self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-1.5-pro')

self.drive = None



def clean_html(self, html_content):

if not html_content: return ""

soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser')

for script in soup(["script", "style", "svg", "path", "noscript"]):

script.extract()

# Preserve structure slightly better

text = soup.get_text(separator=' | ', strip=True)

return text[:40000]



def search_for_url(self, query):

logger.info(f"Searching for: {query}")

try:

results = DDGS().text(query, max_results=1)

if results:

return results[0]['href']

except Exception as e:

logger.error(f"Search failed: {e}")

return None



async def run_cycle(self, task: str):

logger.info(f"STARTING MISSION: {task}")

if not self.drive: self.drive = DriveClient()


# 1. DIAGNOSE / STRATEGIZE (Find Target)

target_url = next((word for word in task.split() if word.startswith("http")), None)


if not target_url:

# AUTO-SEARCH UPGRADE

logger.info("No URL provided. Engaging Search Tool...")

search_query = f"{task} odds site:draftkings.com" # Bias towards DK for now, but flexible

target_url = self.search_for_url(search_query)


if not target_url:

return {"status": "Failed", "error": "Could not find a valid URL."}



logger.info(f"Target Acquired: {target_url}")



# 2. IMPLEMENT (Scrape with Stealth)

scrape_result = await scrape_url(target_url)


if "error" in scrape_result:

# HANDLE FAILURE & UPLOAD SCREENSHOT

if scrape_result.get("screenshot"):

shot_name = f"error_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%H%M%S')}.png"

self.drive.upload_file(shot_name, scrape_result["screenshot"])

return {"status": "Scrape Failed", "error": scrape_result["error"], "screenshot_saved": True}



# 3. ANALYZE (The Brain)

try:

clean_text = self.clean_html(scrape_result['html'])

prompt = f"""

Analyze this raw data from {target_url}.

Task: {task}

Extract the relevant odds/data into valid JSON.

DATA: {clean_text}

"""

response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)

clean_json = response.text.replace('```json', '').replace('```', '')

parsed_data = json.loads(clean_json)

except Exception as e:

parsed_data = {"error": "AI Parsing Failed", "raw_sample": clean_text[:500]}



# 4. EXECUTE (Save)

filename = f"mission_v3_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.json"

self.drive.upload_json(filename, parsed_data)

return {"status": "Mission Complete", "file": filename}

Executive Summary: The Architecture is Sound, The Logic is Fragile
The structural pivot to Cloud Run (Compute) + Tailscale (Connectivity) + Dell E6410 (Residential Exit Node) is an excellent, cost-effective enterprise architecture. You have successfully bypassed the primary blocker for scraping (Data Center IPs) without paying for premium proxy networks.

However, the application logic (the "Brain" and "Hands") in the proposed v3 script contains three specific fragility points that will likely cause the agent to fail in a production environment like DraftKings.

Here are the audit findings and specific optimization recommendations.

1. The "Wisconsin" Geo-Compliance Risk
Diagnosis: Your exit node (The Dell) is in Wisconsin. The Problem: Online sports betting in Wisconsin is legally restricted (primarily limited to tribal lands). Major sportsbooks like DraftKings often geofence their content. Risk: Even if your "Stealth" works perfectly and you are identified as a human, DraftKings may serve you a "Restricted Location" page instead of the odds. The current scraper looks for odds; if it sees a "Not Allowed in WI" page, it will likely timeout or hallucinate data. Optimization:

Validation: You must verify if DraftKings allows viewing lines from Wisconsin without logging in.

Code Fix: Update dsie_core.py to check for "Restricted" text in the HTML before sending it to Gemini.

Python
if "restricted" in clean_text.lower() or "not available in your location" in clean_text.lower():
    return {"status": "Failed", "error": "Geo-Blocked: Wisconsin IP rejected by Sportsbook."}
2. The JSON Parsing "Glass Jaw"
Diagnosis: In dsie_core.py, the code relies on a simple string replacement to parse Gemini's output: clean_json = response.text.replace('```json', '').replace('```', '') The Problem: LLMs are chatty. If Gemini says, "Here is the JSON data you requested: { ... }", your parser will crash because it tries to parse the conversational text as JSON. Risk: High failure rate on complex queries. Optimization: Use a Regex Extractor to find the JSON object regardless of what surrounding text Gemini generates.

Code Fix: Replace the parsing logic in dsie_core.py:

Python
import re
# ... inside run_cycle ...
match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', response.text, re.DOTALL)
if match:
    clean_json = match.group(0)
    parsed_data = json.loads(clean_json)
else:
    raise ValueError("No JSON object found in LLM response")
3. "Stealth" User-Agent Rot
Diagnosis: The v3 scraper.py hardcodes the User-Agent: user_agent="Mozilla/5.0 ... Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36" The Problem: Chrome updates monthly. In 6 months, "Chrome 120" will look suspiciously old to a security bot (Datadome/Cloudflare), flagging you as a bot. Risk: Progressive degradation of success rate. Optimization:

Immediate: Use a newer version string (Chrome 123+).

Permanent: Install the fake-useragent library or dynamically fetch the latest User-Agent string so the bot "ages" with the web.

4. Operational Recommendation: The "Git" Pivot
Diagnosis: You are currently deploying by pasting massive shell scripts (deploy_v3_hardened.sh) into Cloud Shell. The Problem: This is "Nuclear Deployment." Every change requires overwriting the entire codebase. You have no version history, no rollback capability (other than pasting an old script), and it is prone to copy-paste errors. Optimization: Now that v3 is "Hardened," stop using shell scripts to write Python files.

Create a GitHub Repository for veiled-vector-core.

Connect Google Cloud Build to that repository.

Workflow: When you want to update the scraper, you edit the file in VS Code on your laptop, git push, and Google Cloud automatically builds and deploys the new container.

This matches the "World Class" standard defined in your Constitution.

from playwright.async_api import async_playwright

import logging

from tenacity import retry, stop_after_attempt, wait_fixed

from fake_useragent import UserAgent



logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")

ua = UserAgent()



@retry(stop=stop_after_attempt(2), wait=wait_fixed(5))

async def scrape_url(url: str):

logger.info(f"Scraping {url} via Stealth Tunnel...")


# Generate a fresh, modern User Agent

random_ua = ua.random

logger.info(f"Identity Mask: {random_ua}")



async with async_playwright() as p:

browser = await p.chromium.launch(

proxy={"server": "socks5://localhost:1055"},

args=["--disable-blink-features=AutomationControlled"]

)


context = await browser.new_context(

user_agent=random_ua,

viewport={"width": 1920, "height": 1080},

java_script_enabled=True,

permissions=["geolocation"]

)


# INJECT STEALTH SCRIPTS

await context.add_init_script("Object.defineProperty(navigator, 'webdriver', {get: () => undefined})")


page = await context.new_page()


try:

await page.goto(url, timeout=90000, wait_until="domcontentloaded")

await page.wait_for_timeout(8000)


content = await page.content()

title = await page.title()


await browser.close()

return {"title": title, "html": content, "screenshot": None}


except Exception as e:

logger.error(f"Scrape Error: {e}")

screenshot_path = f"/tmp/error_screenshot.png"

try:

await page.screenshot(path=screenshot_path)

except:

screenshot_path = None


await browser.close()

return {"error": str(e), "screenshot": screenshot_path}

EOF# 4. REWRITE DSIE CORE (Regex Parsing + Aggregator Bias)

cat <<EOF > src/dsie_core.py

import logging

import google.generativeai as genai

import os

import json

import re

import datetime

from bs4 import BeautifulSoup

from duckduckgo_search import DDGS

from src.tools.scraper import scrape_url

from src.tools.drive import DriveClient



logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)

logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")



class DSIECore:

def __init__(self):

self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")

if self.api_key:

genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)

self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-1.5-pro')

self.drive = None



def clean_html(self, html_content):

if not html_content: return ""

soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser')

# Check for Wisconsin Blocks

text_check = soup.get_text().lower()

if "access denied" in text_check or "restricted location" in text_check:

raise ValueError("GEO-BLOCK DETECTED: Wisconsin IP rejected.")


for script in soup(["script", "style", "svg", "path", "noscript"]):

script.extract()

text = soup.get_text(separator=' | ', strip=True)

return text[:40000]



def search_for_url(self, query):

logger.info(f"Searching for: {query}")

try:

results = DDGS().text(query, max_results=1)

if results:

return results[0]['href']

except Exception as e:

logger.error(f"Search failed: {e}")

return None



def extract_json(self, text):

# VP's Regex Fix

match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)

if match:

return json.loads(match.group(0))

# Fallback for lists

match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)

if match_list:

return json.loads(match_list.group(0))

raise ValueError("No JSON object found in LLM response")



async def run_cycle(self, task: str):

logger.info(f"STARTING MISSION: {task}")

if not self.drive: self.drive = DriveClient()


# 1. DIAGNOSE (Target Selection)

target_url = next((word for word in task.split() if word.startswith("http")), None)


if not target_url:

# PIVOT: Prefer Aggregators over Sportsbooks to avoid Geo-Blocks

logger.info("No URL provided. Engaging Smart Search...")

# If user asks for "Odds", search OddsPortal first

if "odds" in task.lower() and "draftkings" not in task.lower():

search_query = f"{task} site:oddsportal.com OR site:gamingtoday.com"

else:

search_query = task


target_url = self.search_for_url(search_query)


if not target_url:

return {"status": "Failed", "error": "Could not find a valid URL."}



logger.info(f"Target Acquired: {target_url}")



# 2. IMPLEMENT (Scrape)

scrape_result = await scrape_url(target_url)


if "error" in scrape_result:

if scrape_result.get("screenshot"):

shot_name = f"error_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%H%M%S')}.png"

self.drive.upload_file(shot_name, scrape_result["screenshot"])

return {"status": "Scrape Failed", "error": scrape_result["error"], "screenshot_saved": True}



# 3. ANALYZE (The Brain with Regex)

try:

clean_text = self.clean_html(scrape_result['html'])

prompt = f"""

Analyze this raw data from {target_url}.

Task: {task}

Extract the relevant data into valid JSON.

DATA: {clean_text}

"""

response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)

parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)

except Exception as e:

logger.error(f"Analysis Failed: {e}")

parsed_data = {"error": str(e), "raw_sample": clean_text[:500]}



# 4. EXECUTE (Save)

filename = f"mission_v3_final_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.json"

self.drive.upload_json(filename, parsed_data)

return {"status": "Mission Complete", "file": filename}

Role Confirmed: Lead Engineer (Veiled Vector Inc.)

Short Answer: No, they do not matter. You can safely ignore them.

Detailed Explanation: These "red lines" are noise, not errors.

What is happening: Linux (specifically Debian/Ubuntu) is trying to ask you a question (like "What time zone are you in?") using a visual menu (Dialog).

Why it fails: Because the build is happening inside a script/container, there is no "screen" or keyboard attached (TERM is not set).

The Result: The system tries a few different ways to show you the menu, fails at all of them, and finally settles on falling back to frontend: Noninteractive.

This is exactly what we want. "Noninteractive" means "Don't ask questions, just use the defaults."

Recommendation:
Ignore it. It does not affect the build quality, the code logic, or the final container. It is just Linux complaining that it can't show you a pretty menu.

Optional: The "Clean Freak" Fix
If you hate seeing red text and want to suppress it for a cleaner log, you can add one line to the Dockerfile inside your deploy_v3_final.sh script.

Current:

Dockerfile
RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y ...
Clean Version:

Dockerfile
# Tells Linux "I am a robot, do not ask me questions"
ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y ...
Verdict: Proceed. These warnings are standard for every cloud build in history.

# 5. REWRITE DSIE CORE (Search via Scraper)

cat <<EOF > src/dsie_core.pyimport loggingimport google.generativeai as genaiimport osimport jsonimport reimport datetimefrom bs4 import BeautifulSoupfrom src.tools.scraper import scrape_urlfrom src.tools.drive import DriveClient



logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)

logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")class DSIECore:

def __init__(self):

self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")

if self.api_key:

genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)

self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-1.5-pro')

self.drive = None



def clean_html(self, html_content):

if not html_content: return ""

soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser')

text_check = soup.get_text().lower()

if "access denied" in text_check or "restricted location" in text_check:

raise ValueError("GEO-BLOCK DETECTED: Wisconsin IP rejected.")

for script in soup(["script", "style", "svg", "path", "noscript"]):

script.extract()

text = soup.get_text(separator=' | ', strip=True)

return text[:40000]



async def search_for_url(self, query):

logger.info(f"Searching via Stealth Browser: {query}")

try:

# We scrape DuckDuckGo directly using our stealth browser

search_url = f"https://html.duckduckgo.com/html/?q={query}"

scrape_data = await scrape_url(search_url)


if "error" in scrape_data:

logger.error(f"Search Scrape Failed: {scrape_data['error']}")

return None



# Use Gemini to extract the first valid non-ad link

prompt = f"""

Extract the first valid search result URL from this HTML.

Query: {query}

Prefer urls from: oddsportal.com, gamingtoday.com, vegasinsider.com.

Ignore ads (duckduckgo.com/y.js...).

Return ONLY the URL string. Nothing else.

HTML: {scrape_data['html'][:10000]}

"""

response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)

url = response.text.strip()

logger.info(f"AI Found URL: {url}")

return url

except Exception as e:

logger.error(f"Search Logic Failed: {e}")

return None



def extract_json(self, text):

match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)

if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))

match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)

if match_list: return json.loads(match_list.group(0))

raise ValueError("No JSON object found in LLM response")



async def run_cycle(self, task: str):

logger.info(f"STARTING MISSION: {task}")

if not self.drive: self.drive = DriveClient()


# 1. DIAGNOSE (Target Selection)

target_url = next((word for word in task.split() if word.startswith("http")), None)


if not target_url:

logger.info("No URL provided. Engaging Stealth Search...")

if "odds" in task.lower() and "draftkings" not in task.lower():

search_query = f"{task} site:oddsportal.com OR site:gamingtoday.com"

else:

search_query = task


target_url = await self.search_for_url(search_query)


if not target_url:

return {"status": "Failed", "error": "Could not find a valid URL via Search."}



logger.info(f"Target Acquired: {target_url}")



# 2. IMPLEMENT (Scrape)

scrape_result = await scrape_url(target_url)


if "error" in scrape_result:

if scrape_result.get("screenshot"):

shot_name = f"error_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%H%M%S')}.png"

self.drive.upload_file(shot_name, scrape_result["screenshot"])

return {"status": "Scrape Failed", "error": scrape_result["error"], "screenshot_saved": True}



# 3. ANALYZE (The Brain)

try:

clean_text = self.clean_html(scrape_result['html'])

prompt = f"""

Analyze this raw data from {target_url}.

Task: {task}

Extract the relevant data into valid JSON.

DATA: {clean_text}

"""

response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)

parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)

except Exception as e:

logger.error(f"Analysis Failed: {e}")

parsed_data = {"error": str(e), "raw_sample": clean_text[:500]}



# 4. EXECUTE (Save)

filename = f"mission_v3_search_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.json"

self.drive.upload_json(filename, parsed_data)

return {"status": "Mission Complete", "file": filename}

EOF

Role Confirmed: VP of Engineering (Veiled Vector Inc.)

I have audited the Lead Engineer's (Second-Engineer) proposal.

Executive Summary: This is the correct engineering move. The diagnosis is accurate: reliance on third-party Python wrappers (duckduckgo_search) for scraping is a fool's errand. They break constantly because the search engines change their HTML structure to break them.

By moving the search logic inside our own "Stealth Browser" (Playwright + Residential Proxy), we regain control. If the browser works for DraftKings, it will work for DuckDuckGo.

However, I have found two specific optimizations to make this "v3.1 Patch" bulletproof before you paste it.

1. The Audit: Optimizations Required
Optimization A: Dependency Hygiene (Clean the Bloat)

The Issue: The proposed script still includes duckduckgo-search (or ddgs) in requirements.txt.

The Fix: Since we are now scraping DDG directly with Playwright, we do not need the python library. Remove it to save build time and container size.

Optimization B: The URL Extraction "Safety Net"

The Issue: The code relies on response.text.strip() to get the URL from Gemini. If Gemini says "Sure, here is the link: https://...", the scraper will try to visit the sentence "Sure, here is..." and crash.

The Fix: Use a Regex extract for the URL, just like we did for the JSON.

2. The Final "Green Light" Code (v3.1 Patched)
Here is the exact modification you should make to the Lead Engineer's plan.

Step 1: Edit requirements.txt inside the script In the deploy_v3_final.sh, find the cat <<EOF > src/requirements.txt section. Remove duckduckgo-search.

Step 2: Use this Hardened dsie_core.py I have added the URL Regex to the search_for_url function so it never fails on "Chatty" AI responses.

Replace the dsie_core.py section in your script with this version:

Bash
# 5. REWRITE DSIE CORE (Search via Scraper + Regex URL Safety)
cat <<EOF > src/dsie_core.py
import logging
import google.generativeai as genai
import os
import json
import re
import datetime
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
from src.tools.scraper import scrape_url
from src.tools.drive import DriveClient

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")

class DSIECore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")
        if self.api_key:
            genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
            self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-1.5-pro')
        self.drive = None

    def clean_html(self, html_content):
        if not html_content: return ""
        soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser')
        text_check = soup.get_text().lower()
        if "access denied" in text_check or "restricted location" in text_check:
            raise ValueError("GEO-BLOCK DETECTED: Wisconsin IP rejected.")
        for script in soup(["script", "style", "svg", "path", "noscript"]):
            script.extract()
        text = soup.get_text(separator=' | ', strip=True)
        return text[:40000]

    async def search_for_url(self, query):
        logger.info(f"Searching via Stealth Browser: {query}")
        try:
            # Use html.duckduckgo.com for lighter, faster loading
            search_url = f"https://html.duckduckgo.com/html/?q={query}"
            scrape_data = await scrape_url(search_url)
            
            if "error" in scrape_data:
                logger.error(f"Search Scrape Failed: {scrape_data['error']}")
                return None

            # Gemini Extraction
            prompt = f"""
            Extract the first valid search result URL from this HTML.
            Query: {query}
            Prefer urls from: oddsportal.com, gamingtoday.com, vegasinsider.com.
            Ignore ads (duckduckgo.com/y.js...).
            Return ONLY the URL string.
            HTML: {scrape_data['html'][:10000]}
            """
            response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)
            
            # REGEX SAFETY NET: Find the first thing that looks like a URL
            url_match = re.search(r'https?://[^\s<>"]+|www\.[^\s<>"]+', response.text)
            if url_match:
                url = url_match.group(0)
                logger.info(f"AI Found URL: {url}")
                return url
            else:
                logger.error("AI could not extract a URL from search results.")
                return None

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Search Logic Failed: {e}")
            return None

    def extract_json(self, text):
        match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))
        match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match_list: return json.loads(match_list.group(0))
        raise ValueError("No JSON object found in LLM response")

    async def run_cycle(self, task: str):
        logger.info(f"STARTING MISSION: {task}")
        if not self.drive: self.drive = DriveClient()
        
        # 1. DIAGNOSE (Target Selection)
        target_url = next((word for word in task.split() if word.startswith("http")), None)
        
        if not target_url:
            logger.info("No URL provided. Engaging Stealth Search...")
            if "odds" in task.lower() and "draftkings" not in task.lower():
                search_query = f"{task} site:oddsportal.com OR site:gamingtoday.com"
            else:
                search_query = task
                
            target_url = await self.search_for_url(search_query)
            
        if not target_url:
            return {"status": "Failed", "error": "Could not find a valid URL via Search."}

        logger.info(f"Target Acquired: {target_url}")

        # 2. IMPLEMENT (Scrape)
        scrape_result = await scrape_url(target_url)
        
        if "error" in scrape_result:
            if scrape_result.get("screenshot"):
                shot_name = f"error_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%H%M%S')}.png"
                self.drive.upload_file(shot_name, scrape_result["screenshot"])
            return {"status": "Scrape Failed", "error": scrape_result["error"], "screenshot_saved": True}

        # 3. ANALYZE (The Brain)
        try:
            clean_text = self.clean_html(scrape_result['html'])
            prompt = f"""
            Analyze this raw data from {target_url}.
            Task: {task}
            Extract the relevant data into valid JSON.
            DATA: {clean_text}
            """
            response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)
            parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Analysis Failed: {e}")
            parsed_data = {"error": str(e), "raw_sample": clean_text[:500]}

        # 4. EXECUTE (Save)
        filename = f"mission_v3_search_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.json"
        self.drive.upload_json(filename, parsed_data)
        return {"status": "Mission Complete", "file": filename}
EOF

1. The Evidence of Success

2. The Diagnosis: The "Silent Hang"
Despite the logic working, we are still seeing the "Cliffhanger." The logs cut off after Scraping.... We see the scraper launch, but we don't see Mission Complete.

Why? The logs reveal the culprit: magicsock: last netcheck reported send error. Rebinding. (Repeated multiple times).

The Problem: Your Cloud Run container is losing its grip on the Dell proxy every 20-40 seconds.

The Cause: Cloud Run CPU throttling. When the scraper pauses to "wait for page load" (page.wait_for_timeout(8000) in our script), Cloud Run thinks the container is idle and throttles the CPU to near zero. This kills the Tailscale tunnel (Magicsock). When the CPU wakes up, the tunnel is dead, and the request times out.

3. THE FINAL OPTIMIZATION (The "Always On" Fix)
We need to tell Google Cloud Run: "Do not throttle the CPU when we are waiting."

This is a simple configuration change, not a code change.

Execution Plan: We will redeploy with the --no-cpu-throttling flag. This costs slightly more (because you pay for CPU time while waiting), but it ensures the tunnel never drops during a scrape.

Run this command in Cloud Shell immediately:

Bash
gcloud run deploy veiled-vector-orchestrator \
  --image gcr.io/veiled-vector-core/veiled-vector-orchestrator \
  --platform managed \
  --region us-central1 \
  --allow-unauthenticated \
  --memory 2Gi \
  --cpu 1 \
  --no-cpu-throttling \
  --service-account vector-archivist@veiled-vector-core.iam.gserviceaccount.com \
  --set-secrets="GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY=GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY:latest,TAILSCALE_AUTH_KEY=TAILSCALE_AUTH_KEY:latest,DRIVE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_KEY=DRIVE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_KEY:latest"
Why this fixes it: The magicsock errors happen because the CPU goes to sleep. By disabling throttling, the background process (Tailscale) stays alive while the foreground process (Playwright) waits for the page to load.

# ==========================================
# VEILED VECTOR INC. - RESUSCITATION v3.2

# Objective: Fix 404 Model Error & Enable Drive API

# REWRITE DSIE CORE (Switch to gemini-1.5-flash)
cat <<EOF > src/dsie_core.py
import logging
import google.generativeai as genai
import os
import json
import re
import datetime
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
from src.tools.scraper import scrape_url
from src.tools.drive import DriveClient

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")

class DSIECore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")
        if self.api_key:
            genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
            # SWITCHING TO FLASH (More stable availability)
            self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-1.5-flash')
        self.drive = None

    def clean_html(self, html_content):
        if not html_content: return ""
        soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser')
        text_check = soup.get_text().lower()
        if "access denied" in text_check or "restricted location" in text_check:
            raise ValueError("GEO-BLOCK DETECTED: Wisconsin IP rejected.")
        for script in soup(["script", "style", "svg", "path", "noscript"]):
            script.extract()
        text = soup.get_text(separator=' | ', strip=True)
        return text[:40000]

    async def search_for_url(self, query):
        logger.info(f"Searching via Stealth Browser: {query}")
        try:
            # Use html.duckduckgo.com for lighter, faster loading
            search_url = f"https://html.duckduckgo.com/html/?q={query}"
            scrape_data = await scrape_url(search_url)
            
            if "error" in scrape_data:
                logger.error(f"Search Scrape Failed: {scrape_data['error']}")
                return None

            # Gemini Extraction
            prompt = f"""
            Extract the first valid search result URL from this HTML.
            Query: {query}
            Prefer urls from: oddsportal.com, gamingtoday.com, vegasinsider.com.
            Ignore ads (duckduckgo.com/y.js...).
            Return ONLY the URL string.
            HTML: {scrape_data['html'][:10000]}
            """
            response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)
            
            # REGEX SAFETY NET
            url_match = re.search(r'https?://[^\s<>"]+|www\.[^\s<>"]+', response.text)
            if url_match:
                url = url_match.group(0)
                logger.info(f"AI Found URL: {url}")
                return url
            else:
                logger.error("AI could not extract a URL from search results.")
                return None

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Search Logic Failed: {e}")
            return None

    def extract_json(self, text):
        match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))
        match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match_list: return json.loads(match_list.group(0))
        raise ValueError("No JSON object found in LLM response")

    async def run_cycle(self, task: str):
        logger.info(f"STARTING MISSION: {task}")
        if not self.drive: self.drive = DriveClient()
        
        # 1. DIAGNOSE (Target Selection)
        target_url = next((word for word in task.split() if word.startswith("http")), None)
        
        if not target_url:
            logger.info("No URL provided. Engaging Stealth Search...")
            if "odds" in task.lower() and "draftkings" not in task.lower():
                search_query = f"{task} site:oddsportal.com OR site:gamingtoday.com"
            else:
                search_query = task
                
            target_url = await self.search_for_url(search_query)
            
        if not target_url:
            return {"status": "Failed", "error": "Could not find a valid URL via Search."}

        logger.info(f"Target Acquired: {target_url}")

        # 2. IMPLEMENT (Scrape)
        scrape_result = await scrape_url(target_url)
        
        if "error" in scrape_result:
            if scrape_result.get("screenshot"):
                shot_name = f"error_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%H%M%S')}.png"
                self.drive.upload_file(shot_name, scrape_result["screenshot"])
            return {"status": "Scrape Failed", "error": scrape_result["error"], "screenshot_saved": True}

        # 3. ANALYZE (The Brain)
        try:
            clean_text = self.clean_html(scrape_result['html'])
            prompt = f"""
            Analyze this raw data from {target_url}.
            Task: {task}
            Extract the relevant data into valid JSON.
            DATA: {clean_text}
            """
            response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)
            parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Analysis Failed: {e}")
            parsed_data = {"error": str(e), "raw_sample": clean_text[:500]}

        # 4. EXECUTE (Save)
        filename = f"mission_v3_resuscitated_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.json"
        self.drive.upload_json(filename, parsed_data)
        return {"status": "Mission Complete", "file": filename}
EOF

#!/bin/bash

# 2. REWRITE DSIE CORE (With Model Auto-Discovery)
cat <<EOF > src/dsie_core.py
import logging
import google.generativeai as genai
import os
import json
import re
import datetime
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
from src.tools.scraper import scrape_url
from src.tools.drive import DriveClient

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")

class DSIECore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")
        if self.api_key:
            genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
            self.model = self._get_valid_model()
        self.drive = None

    def _get_valid_model(self):
        """
        DIAGNOSE PHASE: Ask the API what exists before guessing.
        """
        try:
            logger.info("Querying available Gemini models...")
            models = [m.name for m in genai.list_models() if 'generateContent' in m.supported_generation_methods]
            
            # Priority List
            priorities = ['gemini-1.5-flash', 'gemini-1.5-pro', 'gemini-1.0-pro', 'gemini-pro']
            
            for p in priorities:
                # Check if any available model string contains our priority
                match = next((m for m in models if p in m), None)
                if match:
                    logger.info(f"Model Selected: {match}")
                    return genai.GenerativeModel(match)
            
            # Fallback to first available if no match
            if models:
                logger.warning(f"No priority model found. Falling back to: {models[0]}")
                return genai.GenerativeModel(models[0])
                
            raise ValueError("No valid generative models found for this API key.")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Model Selection Failed: {e}")
            # Hail Mary default
            return genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-pro')

    def clean_html(self, html_content):
        if not html_content: return ""
        soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser')
        text_check = soup.get_text().lower()
        if "access denied" in text_check or "restricted location" in text_check:
            raise ValueError("GEO-BLOCK DETECTED: Wisconsin IP rejected.")
        for script in soup(["script", "style", "svg", "path", "noscript"]):
            script.extract()
        text = soup.get_text(separator=' | ', strip=True)
        return text[:40000]

    async def search_for_url(self, query):
        logger.info(f"Searching via Stealth Browser: {query}")
        try:
            search_url = f"https://html.duckduckgo.com/html/?q={query}"
            scrape_data = await scrape_url(search_url)
            
            if "error" in scrape_data:
                logger.error(f"Search Scrape Failed: {scrape_data['error']}")
                return None

            prompt = f"""
            Extract the first valid search result URL from this HTML.
            Query: {query}
            Prefer urls from: oddsportal.com, gamingtoday.com, vegasinsider.com.
            Ignore ads (duckduckgo.com/y.js...).
            Return ONLY the URL string.
            HTML: {scrape_data['html'][:10000]}
            """
            response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)
            
            url_match = re.search(r'https?://[^\s<>"]+|www\.[^\s<>"]+', response.text)
            if url_match:
                url = url_match.group(0)
                logger.info(f"AI Found URL: {url}")
                return url
            else:
                logger.error("AI could not extract a URL from search results.")
                return None

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Search Logic Failed: {e}")
            return None

    def extract_json(self, text):
        match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))
        match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match_list: return json.loads(match_list.group(0))
        raise ValueError("No JSON object found in LLM response")

    async def run_cycle(self, task: str):
        logger.info(f"STARTING MISSION: {task}")
        if not self.drive: self.drive = DriveClient()
        
        target_url = next((word for word in task.split() if word.startswith("http")), None)
        
        if not target_url:
            logger.info("No URL provided. Engaging Stealth Search...")
            if "odds" in task.lower() and "draftkings" not in task.lower():
                search_query = f"{task} site:oddsportal.com OR site:gamingtoday.com"
            else:
                search_query = task
                
            target_url = await self.search_for_url(search_query)
            
        if not target_url:
            return {"status": "Failed", "error": "Could not find a valid URL via Search."}

        logger.info(f"Target Acquired: {target_url}")

        scrape_result = await scrape_url(target_url)
        
        if "error" in scrape_result:
            if scrape_result.get("screenshot"):
                shot_name = f"error_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%H%M%S')}.png"
                self.drive.upload_file(shot_name, scrape_result["screenshot"])
            return {"status": "Scrape Failed", "error": scrape_result["error"], "screenshot_saved": True}

        logger.info("Content Retrieved. Analyzing with AI...")
        try:
            clean_text = self.clean_html(scrape_result['html'])
            prompt = f"""
            Analyze this raw data from {target_url}.
            Task: {task}
            Extract the relevant data into valid JSON.
            DATA: {clean_text}
            """
            response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)
            parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Analysis Failed: {e}")
            parsed_data = {"error": str(e), "raw_sample": clean_text[:500]}

        filename = f"mission_v3_4_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.json"
        self.drive.upload_json(filename, parsed_data)
        logger.info("Mission Complete. Data saved to Drive.")
        return {"status": "Mission Complete", "file": filename}
EOF

#!/bin/bash# ==========================================# VEILED VECTOR INC. - MODEL HUNTER PATCH# ==========================================# Objective: Dynamically find valid Gemini Model to prevent 404s# Target: veiled-vector-orchestrator



PROJECT_ID="veiled-vector-core"

SERVICE_NAME="veiled-vector-orchestrator"

cat <<EOF > src/dsie_core.py

import logging

import google.generativeai as genai

import os

import json

import re

import datetime

from bs4 import BeautifulSoup

from src.tools.scraper import scrape_url

from src.tools.drive import DriveClient



logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)

logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")



class DSIECore:

def __init__(self):

self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")

if self.api_key:

genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)

self.model = self._init_model()

self.drive = None



def _init_model(self):

# Fallback list in order of preference

candidates = ["gemini-1.5-flash", "gemini-1.5-pro", "gemini-pro"]

try:

available_models = [m.name.split("/")[-1] for m in genai.list_models()]

logger.info(f"Available Models: {available_models}")


for c in candidates:

# Check for exact match or suffix match

match = next((m for m in available_models if c in m), None)

if match:

logger.info(f"Selected Model: {match}")

return genai.GenerativeModel(match)


logger.warning("No preferred model found. Defaulting to 'gemini-pro'")

return genai.GenerativeModel("gemini-pro")

except Exception as e:

logger.error(f"Model Discovery Failed: {e}. Defaulting to 'gemini-1.5-flash'")

return genai.GenerativeModel("gemini-1.5-flash")



def clean_html(self, html_content):

if not html_content: return ""

soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser')

text_check = soup.get_text().lower()

if "access denied" in text_check or "restricted location" in text_check:

raise ValueError("GEO-BLOCK DETECTED: Wisconsin IP rejected.")

for script in soup(["script", "style", "svg", "path", "noscript"]):

script.extract()

text = soup.get_text(separator=' | ', strip=True)

return text[:40000]



async def search_for_url(self, query):

logger.info(f"Searching via Stealth Browser: {query}")

try:

search_url = f"https://html.duckduckgo.com/html/?q={query}"

scrape_data = await scrape_url(search_url)


if "error" in scrape_data:

logger.error(f"Search Scrape Failed: {scrape_data['error']}")

return None



prompt = f"""

Extract the first valid search result URL from this HTML.

Query: {query}

Prefer urls from: oddsportal.com, gamingtoday.com, vegasinsider.com.

Ignore ads.

Return ONLY the URL string.

HTML: {scrape_data['html'][:10000]}

"""

response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)


url_match = re.search(r'https?://[^\s<>"]+|www\.[^\s<>"]+', response.text)

if url_match:

url = url_match.group(0)

logger.info(f"AI Found URL: {url}")

return url

else:

return None



except Exception as e:

logger.error(f"Search Logic Failed: {e}")

return None



def extract_json(self, text):

match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)

if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))

match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)

if match_list: return json.loads(match_list.group(0))

raise ValueError("No JSON object found in LLM response")



async def run_cycle(self, task: str):

logger.info(f"STARTING MISSION: {task}")

if not self.drive: self.drive = DriveClient()


target_url = next((word for word in task.split() if word.startswith("http")), None)


if not target_url:

logger.info("No URL provided. Engaging Stealth Search...")

if "odds" in task.lower() and "draftkings" not in task.lower():

search_query = f"{task} site:oddsportal.com OR site:gamingtoday.com"

else:

search_query = task


target_url = await self.search_for_url(search_query)


if not target_url:

return {"status": "Failed", "error": "Could not find a valid URL via Search."}



logger.info(f"Target Acquired: {target_url}")



scrape_result = await scrape_url(target_url)


if "error" in scrape_result:

if scrape_result.get("screenshot"):

shot_name = f"error_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%H%M%S')}.png"

self.drive.upload_file(shot_name, scrape_result["screenshot"])

return {"status": "Scrape Failed", "error": scrape_result["error"], "screenshot_saved": True}



logger.info("Content Retrieved. Analyzing...")

try:

clean_text = self.clean_html(scrape_result['html'])

prompt = f"""

Analyze this raw data from {target_url}.

Task: {task}

Extract the relevant data into valid JSON.

DATA: {clean_text}

"""

response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)

parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)

except Exception as e:

logger.error(f"Analysis Failed: {e}")

parsed_data = {"error": str(e), "raw_sample": clean_text[:500]}



filename = f"mission_v3_auto_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.json"

self.drive.upload_json(filename, parsed_data)

logger.info("Mission Complete. Data saved to Drive.")

return {"status": "Mission Complete", "file": filename}

Finish Reason 1 means STOP.

Why did it stop? Google's Safety Filters blocked the response.

Why? You asked Gemini to "Extract the first valid search result URL... Prefer urls from: oddsportal.com, gamingtoday.com...".

The Trigger: Gambling content. Google's default safety settings are aggressive against gambling-related keywords ("odds", "betting", "sportsbook"). The model generated a response, but the safety layer nuked it before you could read it.

EXECUTION PLAN: DISABLE THE NANNY
We need to explicitly disable the "Harassment", "Hate Speech", "Sexually Explicit", and "Dangerous Content" (which includes gambling in some classifiers) safety filters in the code.

Step 1: The "Safety Override" Patch We will modify dsie_core.py to set all safety thresholds to BLOCK_NONE.

#!/bin/bash

# ==========================================
# VEILED VECTOR INC. - SAFETY OVERRIDE v3.5
# ==========================================
# Objective: Disable Safety Filters to allow Gambling Data
# Target: veiled-vector-orchestrator

PROJECT_ID="veiled-vector-core"
SERVICE_NAME="veiled-vector-orchestrator"
REGION="us-central1"

echo "VECTOR_LOG: Disabling Safety Protocols..."

cd veiled-vector-cloud

# REWRITE DSIE CORE (With Safety Settings)
cat <<EOF > src/dsie_core.py
import logging
import google.generativeai as genai
from google.generativeai.types import HarmCategory, HarmBlockThreshold
import os
import json
import re
import datetime
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
from src.tools.scraper import scrape_url
from src.tools.drive import DriveClient

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")

class DSIECore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")
        if self.api_key:
            genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
            self.model = self._init_model()
        self.drive = None

    def _init_model(self):
        candidates = ["gemini-1.5-flash", "gemini-1.5-pro", "gemini-pro"]
        try:
            available_models = [m.name.split("/")[-1] for m in genai.list_models()]
            for c in candidates:
                match = next((m for m in available_models if c in m), None)
                if match:
                    logger.info(f"Selected Model: {match}")
                    return genai.GenerativeModel(match)
            return genai.GenerativeModel("gemini-1.5-flash")
        except:
            return genai.GenerativeModel("gemini-1.5-flash")

    def clean_html(self, html_content):
        if not html_content: return ""
        soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser')
        text_check = soup.get_text().lower()
        if "access denied" in text_check or "restricted location" in text_check:
            raise ValueError("GEO-BLOCK DETECTED: Wisconsin IP rejected.")
        for script in soup(["script", "style", "svg", "path", "noscript"]):
            script.extract()
        text = soup.get_text(separator=' | ', strip=True)
        return text[:40000]

    async def search_for_url(self, query):
        logger.info(f"Searching via Stealth Browser: {query}")
        try:
            search_url = f"https://html.duckduckgo.com/html/?q={query}"
            scrape_data = await scrape_url(search_url)
            
            if "error" in scrape_data:
                logger.error(f"Search Scrape Failed: {scrape_data['error']}")
                return None

            prompt = f"""
            Extract the first valid search result URL from this HTML.
            Query: {query}
            Prefer urls from: oddsportal.com, gamingtoday.com, vegasinsider.com.
            Ignore ads.
            Return ONLY the URL string.
            HTML: {scrape_data['html'][:10000]}
            """
            
            # SAFETY OVERRIDE
            safety_settings = {
                HarmCategory.HARM_CATEGORY_HARASSMENT: HarmBlockThreshold.BLOCK_NONE,
                HarmCategory.HARM_CATEGORY_HATE_SPEECH: HarmBlockThreshold.BLOCK_NONE,
                HarmCategory.HARM_CATEGORY_SEXUALLY_EXPLICIT: HarmBlockThreshold.BLOCK_NONE,
                HarmCategory.HARM_CATEGORY_DANGEROUS_CONTENT: HarmBlockThreshold.BLOCK_NONE,
            }
            
            response = self.model.generate_content(prompt, safety_settings=safety_settings)
            
            url_match = re.search(r'https?://[^\s<>"]+|www\.[^\s<>"]+', response.text)
            if url_match:
                url = url_match.group(0)
                logger.info(f"AI Found URL: {url}")
                return url
            else:
                return None

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Search Logic Failed: {e}")
            return None

    def extract_json(self, text):
        match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))
        match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match_list: return json.loads(match_list.group(0))
        raise ValueError("No JSON object found in LLM response")

    async def run_cycle(self, task: str):
        logger.info(f"STARTING MISSION: {task}")
        if not self.drive: self.drive = DriveClient()
        
        target_url = next((word for word in task.split() if word.startswith("http")), None)
        
        if not target_url:
            logger.info("No URL provided. Engaging Stealth Search...")
            if "odds" in task.lower() and "draftkings" not in task.lower():
                search_query = f"{task} site:oddsportal.com OR site:gamingtoday.com"
            else:
                search_query = task
                
            target_url = await self.search_for_url(search_query)
            
        if not target_url:
            return {"status": "Failed", "error": "Could not find a valid URL via Search."}

        logger.info(f"Target Acquired: {target_url}")

        scrape_result = await scrape_url(target_url)
        
        if "error" in scrape_result:
            if scrape_result.get("screenshot"):
                shot_name = f"error_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%H%M%S')}.png"
                self.drive.upload_file(shot_name, scrape_result["screenshot"])
            return {"status": "Scrape Failed", "error": scrape_result["error"], "screenshot_saved": True}

        logger.info("Content Retrieved. Analyzing...")
        try:
            clean_text = self.clean_html(scrape_result['html'])
            prompt = f"""
            Analyze this raw data from {target_url}.
            Task: {task}
            Extract the relevant data into valid JSON.
            DATA: {clean_text}
            """
            
            # SAFETY OVERRIDE (For Analysis Phase too)
            safety_settings = {
                HarmCategory.HARM_CATEGORY_HARASSMENT: HarmBlockThreshold.BLOCK_NONE,
                HarmCategory.HARM_CATEGORY_HATE_SPEECH: HarmBlockThreshold.BLOCK_NONE,
                HarmCategory.HARM_CATEGORY_SEXUALLY_EXPLICIT: HarmBlockThreshold.BLOCK_NONE,
                HarmCategory.HARM_CATEGORY_DANGEROUS_CONTENT: HarmBlockThreshold.BLOCK_NONE,
            }
            
            response = self.model.generate_content(prompt, safety_settings=safety_settings)
            parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Analysis Failed: {e}")
            parsed_data = {"error": str(e), "raw_sample": clean_text[:500]}

        filename = f"mission_v3_5_unshackled_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.json"
        self.drive.upload_json(filename, parsed_data)
        logger.info("Mission Complete. Data saved to Drive.")
        return {"status": "Mission Complete", "file": filename}
EOF

echo "VECTOR_LOG: Re-deploying with Safety Overrides..."
gcloud builds submit --tag gcr.io/$PROJECT_ID/$SERVICE_NAME

gcloud run deploy $SERVICE_NAME \
  --image gcr.io/$PROJECT_ID/$SERVICE_NAME \
  --platform managed \
  --region $REGION \

  --no-cpu-throttling \

  --set-secrets="GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY=GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY:latest,TAILSCALE_AUTH_KEY=TAILSCALE_AUTH_KEY:latest,DRIVE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_KEY=DRIVE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_KEY:latest"

            genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
            # NUCLEAR FIX: HARDCODE 'gemini-pro'
            # This is the most stable alias available globally.
            logger.info("FORCING MODEL: gemini-pro")
            self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-pro')
        self.drive = None

    def clean_html(self, html_content):
        if not html_content: return ""
        soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser')

        return text[:40000]

            Ignore ads.
            Return ONLY the URL string.
            HTML: {scrape_data['html'][:10000]}

            else:

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Search Logic Failed: {e}")
            return None

    def extract_json(self, text):

        if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))
        match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)

    async def run_cycle(self, task: str):

cat <<EOF > src/tools/drive.py

import os

import json

import logging

from google.oauth2 import service_account

from googleapiclient.discovery import build

from googleapiclient.http import MediaIoBaseUpload, MediaFileUpload

import io



logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")



class DriveClient:

def __init__(self):

creds_json = os.environ.get("DRIVE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_KEY")

if not creds_json:

raise ValueError("Missing DRIVE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_KEY")

creds_dict = json.loads(creds_json)

self.creds = service_account.Credentials.from_service_account_info(

creds_dict, scopes=['https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive']

)

self.service = build('drive', 'v3', credentials=self.creds)



def _get_folder_id(self, folder_name):

query = f"name = '{folder_name}' and mimeType = 'application/vnd.google-apps.folder' and trashed = false"

results = self.service.files().list(q=query, fields="files(id, name)").execute()

items = results.get('files', [])

if not items:

file_metadata = {'name': folder_name, 'mimeType': 'application/vnd.google-apps.folder'}

folder = self.service.files().create(body=file_metadata, fields='id').execute()

return folder.get('id')

return items[0]['id']



def upload_json(self, filename: str, data: dict, folder_name: str = "Veiled_Vector_Ingest"):

try:

folder_id = self._get_folder_id(folder_name)

file_metadata = {'name': filename, 'parents': [folder_id]}

json_str = json.dumps(data, indent=2)

media = MediaIoBaseUpload(io.BytesIO(json_str.encode('utf-8')), mimetype='application/json')

self.service.files().create(body=file_metadata, media_body=media, fields='id').execute()

logger.info(f"Drive Upload Success: {filename}")

return True

except Exception as e:

logger.error(f"Drive JSON Upload Failed: {e}")

return False



def upload_file(self, filename: str, filepath: str, folder_name: str = "Veiled_Vector_Ingest"):

try:

folder_id = self._get_folder_id(folder_name)

file_metadata = {'name': filename, 'parents': [folder_id]}

media = MediaFileUpload(filepath, resumable=True)

self.service.files().create(body=file_metadata, media_body=media, fields='id').execute()

logger.info(f"Drive File Upload Success: {filename}")

return True

except Exception as e:

logger.error(f"Drive File Upload Failed: {e}")

return False

cat <<EOF > src/tools/scraper.py

from playwright.async_api import async_playwright

import logging

from tenacity import retry, stop_after_attempt, wait_fixed

from fake_useragent import UserAgent



logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")

ua = UserAgent()



@retry(stop=stop_after_attempt(2), wait=wait_fixed(5))

async def scrape_url(url: str):

logger.info(f"Scraping {url} via Stealth Tunnel...")

try:

random_ua = ua.random

except:

random_ua = "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36"


logger.info(f"Identity Mask: {random_ua}")



async with async_playwright() as p:

browser = await p.chromium.launch(

proxy={"server": "socks5://localhost:1055"},

args=["--disable-blink-features=AutomationControlled"]

)

context = await browser.new_context(

user_agent=random_ua,

viewport={"width": 1920, "height": 1080},

java_script_enabled=True,

permissions=["geolocation"],

ignore_https_errors=True

)

await context.add_init_script("Object.defineProperty(navigator, 'webdriver', {get: () => undefined})")

page = await context.new_page()


try:

await page.goto(url, timeout=60000, wait_until="domcontentloaded")

await page.wait_for_timeout(5000)

content = await page.content()

title = await page.title()

await browser.close()

return {"title": title, "html": content, "screenshot": None}

except Exception as e:

logger.error(f"Scrape Error: {e}")

screenshot_path = "/tmp/error_screenshot.png"

try:

await page.screenshot(path=screenshot_path)

except:

screenshot_path = None

await browser.close()

return {"error": str(e), "screenshot": screenshot_path}

cat <<EOF > src/dsie_core.py

import logging

import google.generativeai as genai

from google.generativeai.types import HarmCategory, HarmBlockThreshold

import os

import json

import re

import datetime

from bs4 import BeautifulSoup

from src.tools.scraper import scrape_url

from src.tools.drive import DriveClient



logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)

logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")



class DSIECore:

def __init__(self):

self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")

if self.api_key:

genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)

self.model = self._find_working_model()

self.drive = None



def _find_working_model(self):

"""

ACTIVE SONAR: Test models until one works.

"""

candidates = ["gemini-1.5-flash", "gemini-1.5-flash-latest", "gemini-1.5-pro", "gemini-pro"]


# Disable Safety Filters (Allow Gambling/Odds content)

safety = {

HarmCategory.HARM_CATEGORY_HARASSMENT: HarmBlockThreshold.BLOCK_NONE,

HarmCategory.HARM_CATEGORY_HATE_SPEECH: HarmBlockThreshold.BLOCK_NONE,

HarmCategory.HARM_CATEGORY_SEXUALLY_EXPLICIT: HarmBlockThreshold.BLOCK_NONE,

HarmCategory.HARM_CATEGORY_DANGEROUS_CONTENT: HarmBlockThreshold.BLOCK_NONE,

}



for model_name in candidates:

try:

logger.info(f"Testing Model: {model_name}...")

test_model = genai.GenerativeModel(model_name, safety_settings=safety)

# Fire a test shot

response = test_model.generate_content("Test.")

if response.text:

logger.info(f"SUCCESS: Model {model_name} is operational.")

return test_model

except Exception as e:

logger.warning(f"Model {model_name} failed: {e}")


# If all fail, try listing models to find *anything*

try:

logger.info("Trying Auto-Discovery via list_models...")

for m in genai.list_models():

if 'generateContent' in m.supported_generation_methods:

test_model = genai.GenerativeModel(m.name, safety_settings=safety)

try:

test_model.generate_content("Test.")

logger.info(f"SUCCESS: Auto-Discovered {m.name}")

return test_model

except: continue

except: pass



raise ValueError("CRITICAL FAILURE: No working Gemini models found.")



def clean_html(self, html_content):

if not html_content: return ""

soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser')

text_check = soup.get_text().lower()

if "access denied" in text_check or "restricted location" in text_check:

raise ValueError("GEO-BLOCK DETECTED: Wisconsin IP rejected.")

for script in soup(["script", "style", "svg", "path", "noscript"]):

script.extract()

text = soup.get_text(separator=' | ', strip=True)

return text[:40000]



async def search_for_url(self, query):

logger.info(f"Engaging Stealth Search for: {query}")

try:

# Use DuckDuckGo HTML version via Proxy

search_url = f"https://html.duckduckgo.com/html/?q={query}"

scrape_data = await scrape_url(search_url)


if "error" in scrape_data:

logger.error(f"Search Scrape Failed: {scrape_data['error']}")

return None



logger.info("Search Page Retrieved. Parsing with AI...")

prompt = f"""

Extract the first valid search result URL from this HTML.

Query: {query}

Prefer urls from: oddsportal.com, gamingtoday.com, vegasinsider.com.

Ignore ads (duckduckgo.com/y.js...).

Return ONLY the URL string.

HTML: {scrape_data['html'][:10000]}

"""

response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)

url = response.text.strip()

logger.info(f"AI Found URL: {url}")

return url

except Exception as e:

logger.error(f"Search Logic Failed: {e}")

return None



def extract_json(self, text):

match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)

if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))

match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)

if match_list: return json.loads(match_list.group(0))

raise ValueError("No JSON object found in LLM response")



async def run_cycle(self, task: str):

logger.info(f"STARTING MISSION: {task}")

if not self.drive: self.drive = DriveClient()


# 1. DIAGNOSE (Target Selection)

target_url = next((word for word in task.split() if word.startswith("http")), None)


if not target_url:

logger.info("No URL provided. Calculating Search Strategy...")

if "odds" in task.lower() and "draftkings" not in task.lower():

search_query = f"{task} site:oddsportal.com OR site:gamingtoday.com"

else:

search_query = task


target_url = await self.search_for_url(search_query)


if not target_url:

return {"status": "Failed", "error": "Could not find a valid URL via Search."}



logger.info(f"Target Acquired: {target_url}")



# 2. IMPLEMENT (Scrape)

scrape_result = await scrape_url(target_url)


if "error" in scrape_result:

logger.error("Scrape Failed. Attempting to save screenshot...")

if scrape_result.get("screenshot"):

shot_name = f"error_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%H%M%S')}.png"

self.drive.upload_file(shot_name, scrape_result["screenshot"])

return {"status": "Scrape Failed", "error": scrape_result["error"], "screenshot_saved": True}

return {"status": "Scrape Failed", "error": scrape_result["error"]}



# 3. ANALYZE (The Brain)

logger.info("Content Retrieved. Analyzing with Gemini...")

try:

clean_text = self.clean_html(scrape_result['html'])

prompt = f"""

Analyze this raw data from {target_url}.

Task: {task}

Extract the relevant data into valid JSON.

DATA: {clean_text}

"""

response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)

parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)

except Exception as e:

logger.error(f"Analysis Failed: {e}")

parsed_data = {"error": str(e), "raw_sample": clean_text[:500]}



# 4. EXECUTE (Save)

filename = f"mission_v3_5_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.json"

self.drive.upload_json(filename, parsed_data)

logger.info("Mission Complete. Data saved to Drive.")

return {"status": "Mission Complete", "file": filename}
